class=\"highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=\"class ParticleSystem {\n    constructor(canvas) {\n        this.canvas = canvas;\n        this.ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');\n        this.particles = [];\n        this.init();\n    }\n\n    init() {\n        this.resize();\n        for (let i = 0; i \u0026lt; 50; i++) {\n            this.particles.push({\n                x: Math.random() * this.canvas.width,\n                y: Math.random() * this.canvas.height,\n                vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5,\n                vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5,\n                radius: Math.random() * 2 + 1\n            });\n        }\n        this.animate();\n    }\n\n    animate() {\n        this.ctx.clearRect(0, 0, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);\n        this.particles.forEach(p =\u0026gt; {\n            p.x += p.vx;\n            p.y += p.vy;\n            // Wrap around edges\n            if (p.x \u0026lt; 0) p.x = this.canvas.width;\n            if (p.x \u0026gt; this.canvas.width) p.x = 0;\n            if (p.y \u0026lt; 0) p.y = this.canvas.height;\n            if (p.y \u0026gt; this.canvas.height) p.y = 0;\n            // Draw\n            this.ctx.beginPath();\n            this.ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, p.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);\n data-hpc="true"><article class="markdown-body entry-content container-lg" itemprop="text"><div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h1 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Style Presets <p dir="auto">Curated visual styles for Frontend Slides. Each preset includes specific font choices, color palettes, and animation approaches to ensure distinctive, non-generic designs.</p>
<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Dark Themes</h2><a id="user-content-dark-themes" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Dark Themes" href="#dark-themes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>

    <span class="pl-s1">--text-secondary</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-pds"><span class="pl-kos">#</span>555555</span>;
    <span class="pl-s1">--accent</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-pds"><span class="pl-kos">#</span>ff3300</span>;
    <span class="pl-s1">--grid</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-en">rgba</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.05</span>);
}</pre></div>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Signature Elements:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Visible grid system</li>
<li>Asymmetric layouts</li>
<li>Red accent sparingly</li>
<li>Bold black typography</li>
<li>Geometric shapes</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Animation Style:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Precise, mechanical (0.3-0.4s)</li>
<li>Linear or ease-out easing</li>
<li>Grid-aligned movements</li>
</ul>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Animation Easing Reference</h2><a id="user-content-animation-easing-reference" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Animation Easing Reference" href="#animation-easing-reference"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-css notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=":root {
    /* Standard curves */
    --ease-out-expo: cubic-bezier(0.16, 1, 0.3, 1);
    --ease-out-quart: cubic-bezier(0.25, 1, 0.5, 1);
    --ease-out-cubic: cubic-bezier(0.33, 1, 0.68, 1);

    /* Bouncy */
    --ease-bounce: cubic-bezier(0.34, 1.56, 0.64, 1);
    --ease-spring: cubic-bezier(0.175, 0.885, 0.32, 1.275);

    /* Smooth */
    --ease-smooth: cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);

    /* Snappy */
    --ease-snappy: cubic-bezier(0.68, -0.55, 0.265, 1.55);
}"><pre><span class="pl-kos">:</span><span class="pl-c1">root</span> {
    <span class="pl-c">/* Standard curves */</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">--ease-out-expo</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-en">cubic-bezier</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0.16</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.3</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>);
    <span class="pl-s1">--ease-out-quart</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-en">cubic-bezier</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0.25</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.5</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>);
    <span class="pl-s1">--ease-out-cubic</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-en">cubic-bezier</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0.33</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.68</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>);

    <span class="pl-c">/* Bouncy */</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">--ease-bounce</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-en">cubic-bezier</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0.34</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1.56</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.64</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>);
    <span class="pl-s1">--ease-spring</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-en">cubic-bezier</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0.175</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.885</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.32</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1.275</span>);

    <span class="pl-c">/* Smooth */</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">--ease-smooth</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-en">cubic-bezier</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0.4</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.2</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1</span>);

    <span class="pl-c">/* Snappy */</span>
    <span class="pl-s1">--ease-snappy</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span> <span class="pl-en">cubic-bezier</span>(<span class="pl-c1">0.68</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">-0.55</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.265</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">1.55</span>);
}</pre></div>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Background Effect Snippets</h2><a id="user-content-background-effect-snippets" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Background Effect Snippets" href="#background-effect-snippets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Particle Field (Canvas)</h3><a id="user-content-particle-field-canvas" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Particle Field (Canvas)" href="#particle-field-canvas"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-js notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="class ParticleSystem {
    constructor(canvas) {
        this.canvas = canvas;
        this.ctx = canvas.getContext('2d');
        this.particles = [];
        this.init();
    }

    init() {
        this.resize();
        for (let i = 0; i &lt; 50; i++) {
            this.particles.push({
                x: Math.random() * this.canvas.width,
                y: Math.random() * this.canvas.height,
                vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5,
                vy: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.5,
                radius: Math.random() * 2 + 1
            });
        }
        this.animate();
    }

    animate() {
        this.ctx.clearRect(0, 0, this.canvas.width, this.canvas.height);
        this.particles.forEach(p =&gt; {
            p.x += p.vx;
            p.y += p.vy;
            // Wrap around edges
            if (p.x &lt; 0) p.x = this.canvas.width;
            if (p.x &gt; this.canvas.width) p.x = 0;
            if (p.y &lt; 0) p.y = this.canvas.height;
            if (p.y &gt; this.canvas.height) p.y = 0;
            // Draw
            this.ctx.beginPath();
            this.ctx.arc(p.x, p.y, p.radius, 0, Math.PI * 2);
            this.ctx.fillStyle = 'rgba(0, 255, 204, 0.5)';
            this.ctx.fill();
        });
        requestAnimationFrame(() =&gt; this.animate());
    }
}"><pre><span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">ParticleSystem</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

        <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">init</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>
    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

    <span class="pl-en">init</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>

        <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-k">let</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">0</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span> <span class="pl-c1">&lt;</span> <span class="pl-c1">50</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span> <span class="pl-s1">i</span><span class="pl-c1">++</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">particles</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">push</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">{</span>
                <span class="pl-c1">x</span>: <span class="pl-v">Math</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">random</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-kos">)</span> <span class="pl-c1">*</span> <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">canvas</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">width</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span>

    <span class="pl-kos">}</span>

        <span class="pl-smi">this</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">particles</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-en">forEach</span><span class="pl-kos">(</span><span class="pl-s1">p</span> <span class="pl-c1">=&gt;</span> <span class="pl-kos">{</span>
            <span class="pl-s1">p</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">x</span> <span class="pl-c1">+=</span> <span class="pl-s1">p</span><span class="pl-kos">.</span><span class="pl-c1">vx</span><span class="pl-kos">;</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Gradient Mesh (CSS)</h3><a id="user-content-gradient-mesh-css" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Gradient Mesh (CSS)" href="#gradient-mesh-css"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-css notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=".gradient-mesh {
    background:
        radial-gradient(at 40% 20%, hsla(280, 100%, 70%, 0.3) 0px, transparent 50%),
        radial-gradient(at 80% 0%, hsla(200, 100%, 60%, 0.3) 0px, transparent 50%),
        radial-gradient(at 0% 50%, hsla(340, 100%, 70%, 0.3) 0px, transparent 50%),
        radial-gradient(at 80% 50%, hsla(180, 100%, 50%, 0.2) 0px, transparent 50%),
        radial-gradient(at 0% 100%, hsla(250, 100%, 60%, 0.3) 0px, transparent 50%),
        radial-gradient(at 80% 100%, hsla(20, 100%, 60%, 0.2) 0px, transparent 50%),
        var(--bg-primary);
}"><pre>.<span class="pl-c1">gradient-mesh</span> {
    <span class="pl-c1">background</span><span class="pl-kos">:</span>
        <span class="pl-en">radial-gradient</span>(at <span class="pl-c1">40<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span> <span class="pl-c1">20<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-en">hsla</span>(<span class="pl-c1">280</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">100<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">70<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.3</span>) <span class="pl-c1">0<span class="pl-smi">px</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> transparent <span class="pl-c1">50<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span>)<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-en">radial-gradient</span>(at <span class="pl-c1">80<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span> <span class="pl-c1">0<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-en">hsla</span>(<span class="pl-c1">200</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">100<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">60<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.3</span>) <span class="pl-c1">0<span class="pl-smi">px</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> transparent <span class="pl-c1">50<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span>)<span class="pl-kos">,</span>
        <span class="pl-en">radial-gradient</span>(at <span class="pl-c1">0<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span> <span class="pl-c1">50<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-en">hsla</span>(<span class="pl-c1">340</span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">100<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">70<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">0.3</span>) <span class="pl-c1">0<span class="pl-smi">px</span></span><span class="pl-kos">,</span> transparent <span class="pl-c1">50<span class="pl-smi">%</span></span>)<span class="pl-kos">,</span>

<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h3 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">Noise Texture (SVG Data URI)</h3><a id="user-content-noise-texture-svg-data-uri" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: Noise Texture (SVG Data URI)" href="#noise-texture-svg-data-uri"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-css notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content=".noise {
    background-image: url(&quot;data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg viewBox='0 0 400 400' xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'%3E%3Cfilter id='noiseFilter'%3E%3CfeTurbulence type='fractalNoise' baseFrequency='0.9' numOctaves='3' stitchTiles='stitch'/%3E%3C/filter%3E%3Crect width='100%25' height='100%25' filter='url(%23noiseFilter)'/%3E%3C/svg%3E&quot;);

<hr>
<div class="markdown-heading" dir="auto"><h2 tabindex="-1" class="heading-element" dir="auto">DO NOT USE (Generic AI Patterns)</h2><a id="user-content-do-not-use-generic-ai-patterns" class="anchor" aria-label="Permalink: DO NOT USE (Generic AI Patterns)" href="#do-not-use-generic-ai-patterns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m7.775 3.275 1.25-1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1 4.95 4.95l-2.5 2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1-4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1 .018-1.042.751.751 0 0 1 1.042-.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l2.5-2.5a2.002 2.002 0 0 0-2.83-2.83l-1.25 1.25a.751.751 0 0 1-1.042-.018.751.751 0 0 1-.018-1.042Zm-4.69 9.64a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 2.83 0l1.25-1.25a.751.751 0 0 1 1.042.018.751.751 0 0 1 .018 1.042l-1.25 1.25a3.5 3.5 0 1 1-4.95-4.95l2.5-2.5a3.5 3.5 0 0 1 4.95 0 .751.751 0 0 1-.018 1.042.751.751 0 0 1-1.042.018 1.998 1.998 0 0 0-2.83 0l-2.5 2.5a1.998 1.998 0 0 0 0 2.83Z"></path></svg></a></div>
<p dir="auto">Avoid these overused patterns that create "AI slop":</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Fonts:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Inter (except in Gradient Wave style)</li>
<li>Roboto</li>
<li>Arial / Helvetica</li>
<li>System font stacks as display fonts</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Colors:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li><code>#6366f1</code> (generic indigo)</li>
<li>Purple/violet gradients on white</li>
<li>Generic blue primary buttons</li>
<li>Equal distribution of accent colors</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Layouts:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Centered everything</li>
<li>Generic hero with text left, image right</li>
<li>Standard 3-column features grid</li>
<li>Rounded rectangle cards with shadows</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Animations:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Identical timing on all elements</li>
<li>No stagger on children</li>
<li>Linear easing everywhere</li>
<li>Excessive bounce</li>
</ul>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Effects:</strong></p>
<ul dir="auto">
<li>Drop shadows without intention</li>
<li>Gratuitous glassmorphism</li>
<li>Blurs that don't add meaning</li>
<li>Gradients for no reason</li>
</ul>
</article></div><button hidden=""></button></section></div></div></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> </div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div id="find-result-marks-container" class="Box-sc-62in7e-0 vdPNv"></div><button hidden="" data-testid="" data-hotkey-scope="read-only-cursor-text-area"></button><button hidden=""></button></div> <!-- --> <!-- --> <script type="application/json" id="__PRIMER_DATA__R_0___">{"resolvedServerColorMode":"night"}</script></div>
</react-app>
</turbo-frame>



  </div>

</turbo-frame>

    </main>
  </div>
